sys_gagarin_init = {
    name = "Gagarin"
    class = sc_k
	max_instances = 1
	
	flags = { attican_traverse_system armstrong_nebula_system gagarin_system btr_system custom_system }	
	
	planet = {
		name = "Gagarin"
		class = pc_k_star
        orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = 33
		has_ring = no
		flags = { gagarin_star }	
		init_effect = {
			create_ambient_object = {
				type = "nebula_1"
				entity_offset_height = -5
				location = this
			}
			last_created_ambient_object = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 0
					angle = random
				}
			}
		}		
	}

    planet = {
        name = "Junthor"
        class = pc_chlorine
        orbit_distance = 100
        orbit_angle = 165
        has_ring = no
		size = 25 
		init_effect = {
			add_deposit = d_aluminum_surface
			add_deposit = d_aluminum_surface
			add_deposit = d_aluminum_surface
			add_deposit = d_nickel_deposits
			add_deposit = d_nickel_deposits
			#add_deposit = d_average_mineral_deposits
			add_deposit = d_minerals_5
			add_deposit = d_junthor_ruins			
			add_deposit = d_society_3
			add_deposit = d_engineering_2
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = junthor_codex_untranslated
				days = -1
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = bleak_planet
				days = -1
			}
		}	

		flags = { junthor_planet btr_custom }		

		moon = {
			name = "Junthor a"
			class = pc_iron
			orbit_distance = 20
			size = 5
			init_effect = {
				prevent_anomaly = yes
			}						
		}

		moon = {
			name = "Junthor b"
			class = pc_frozen
			orbit_distance = 5
			size = 3	
			init_effect = {
				prevent_anomaly = yes
				#add_deposit = d_average_iridium_deposits
				#add_deposit = d_average_palladium_deposits
				add_deposit = d_rare_crystals_4
			}				
		}

		moon = {
			name = "Junthor c"
			class = pc_barren
			orbit_distance = 5
			size = 3
			init_effect = {
				prevent_anomaly = yes
				#add_deposit = d_rich_platinum_deposits
				add_deposit = d_rare_crystals_2
			}			
		}		
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Pressha"
        class = pc_ice_giant
        orbit_distance = 100
        orbit_angle = 202
        has_ring = no
		size = 30

		flags = { pressha_planet btr_custom }

			}

				modifier = pressha_codex

			name = "Pressha a"

		moon = {

				prevent_anomaly = yes

				add_deposit = d_rare_crystals_1

    planet = {

			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = rayingri_unsurveyed_codex
				days = -1
			}
		}

		moon = {
			name = "Vahtz"
			class = pc_iron
			orbit_distance = 20
			size = 6	

			flags = { vahtz_planet btr_custom }	

			init_effect = {
				prevent_anomaly = yes					

				add_modifier = {
					modifier = vahtz_unsurveyed_codex
					days = -1
				}	
			}				
		}
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Sogelrus"
        class = pc_frozen
        orbit_distance = 100
        orbit_angle = 286
        has_ring = no
		size = 11

		flags = { sogelrus_planet btr_custom }

		init_effect = {

			add_modifier = {
				modifier = sogelrus_codex
			}
		}
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Antirumgon"
        class = pc_carbon
        orbit_distance = 100
        orbit_angle = 289
        has_ring = no
		size = 23

		flags = { antirumgon_planet btr_custom }	

		init_effect = {
			
			#add_deposit = d_poor_mineral_deposits
			add_deposit = minerals_3
			add_deposit = d_trade_value_1
			add_deposit = d_society_3

			add_modifier = {
				modifier = carbon_world
				days = -1
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = antirumgon_codex
				days = -1
			}
			create_pirate_country = yes
			event_target:pirate_country = {
				create_leader = {
					class = admiral
					species = event_target:batarianSpecies
					name = "Red Qorayk"
					skill = 1
					traits = {
						trait = random_trait
					}
				}				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_modifier = pirate_power
						}
					}
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = pirate_power
						days = -1
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				establish_communications_no_message = event_target:pirate_country
			}
			create_fleet = {
				name = "Pirate Station"
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:pirate_country
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "NAME_Pirate_Nest"
						graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
					}
					set_location = {
						target = prev
						distance = 6
						angle = 120
					}
				}
			}			
			create_fleet = {
				name = "Red's Raiders"
				effect = {
					set_owner = event_target:pirate_country
					set_fleet_flag = pirate_home_system_fleet
					while = {
						count = 1
						create_ship = {
							name = "Khi'shar"
							design = "NAME_Brigand"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 6
						create_ship = {
							name = random
							design = "NAME_Reaver"
							graphical_culture = "pirate_01"
						}
					}
					assign_leader = last_created_leader					
					set_fleet_flag = pirate_home_system_fleet
					set_formation_scale = 2
					set_fleet_stance = aggressive
					set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
					set_aggro_range = 150
					set_location = {
						target = prev
						distance = 10
						angle = 120
					}
				}
			}			
		}			
    }
}
